<h1 class="kt-adv-heading105_f057ff-ba wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_f057ff-ba">Bringing 700+ Quick &amp; Easy International Food Recipes To Your Home</h1>



<p class="kt-adv-heading105_eb9539-b0 has--font-size wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_eb9539-b0">Embark on a flavourful journey with JWD Recipes. Your guide to authentic global cuisine and family-friendly dinner ideas. From comfort food recipes like spicy curries to healthy savory pastas.</p>

<div class="kb-row-layout-wrap kb-row-layout-id105_8fadfa-47 alignnone has-theme-palette7-background-color kt-row-has-bg wp-block-kadence-rowlayout"><div class="kt-row-column-wrap kt-has-2-columns kt-row-layout-equal kt-tab-layout-inherit kt-mobile-layout-row kt-row-valign-middle kb-theme-content-width">

<div class="wp-block-kadence-column kadence-column105_5c0ebe-cb kb-section-dir-vertical"><div class="kt-inside-inner-col">
<p class="kt-adv-heading105_cc882e-04 has--font-size wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-2-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_cc882e-04"><strong>Founder</strong></p>



<h2 class="kt-adv-heading105_e38707-5f wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_e38707-5f">Hello! I&#8217;m Jon Dawson</h2>



<p class="kt-adv-heading105_bbb787-c0 has--font-size wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_bbb787-c0">I founded this food blog driven by my love for cooking and the joy of sharing delightful meals with others.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading105_2763a8-e9 has--font-size wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_2763a8-e9">I have spent countless hours in the kitchen with my wife and our two young daughters, exploring a variety of recipes from different cultures.</p>



<p class="kt-adv-heading105_b767b1-a7 has--font-size wp-block-kadence-advancedheading has-theme-palette-3-color has-text-color" data-kb-block="kb-adv-heading105_b767b1-a7">Those experiences have fostered in me a profound appreciation for food and a passion for encouraging others to find joy in cooking.</p>
